technologies enabling customers discover new ways of using energy, all over the world. 
 
ENEL is a subsidiary fully owned by E NEL SpA. ENEL SpA is a multinational energy company and one of the 
world’s leading integrated electricity and gas operators. Enel SpA works in 37 countries across 5 continents, 
generating energy with a net installed capacity of almost 84 GW, selling gas and distributin g electricity across a 
network spanning approximately 2.1 million km. With around 64 million end users around the world, Enel SpA 
has the biggest customer base among our European competitors, and is one of Europe’s leading energy companies 
by installed capacity and reported EBITDA. Enel SpA’s portfolio of power stations is highly diversified, running 
on hydroelectric, wind, geothermal, solar, thermoelectric, nuclear and other renewable sources of power. Almost 
half of the energy generated by ENEL is produced with zero carbon dioxide emissions, making the group one of 
the leading producers of clean energy. The Enel Group is made up of nearly 70,000 people from around the world 
whose brilliant work is based on values of Responsibility, Innovation, Trust and Pr oactivity. Together all Enel 
Group employees are working on the same goal of “Open Power” in order to tackle some of the world’s greatest 
challenges. Within the strategy of opening electricity to new uses, towards the end of 2017 Enel SpA restructured 
its organisation creating Enel X, a subsidiary dedicated to non -commodity activities such as energy efficiency, 
demand response, smart cities, smart homes and electric mobility. 
 
ENEL is currently involved as subsidiary of Enel SpA into the development of H2020 and CEF funded programs 
such as EVA+ ‘Electric Vehicles Arteries in Italy and Austria’ co-financed by the European Union's Connecting 
Europe Facility. Prior to the involvement in Study with Pilots / Works Action related to EV charging infrastructure, 
ENEL developed its own portfolio of EV charging stations that allowed to execute design -to-cost activities to 
maximize the financial sustainability of the charging infrastructure investment and are currently outsourced to a 
EU-wide pool of manufacturing suppliers (for Normal and Fast charging stations).

1. Enel Info+ Project [Other]: Enel Info+ is a large-scale trial of the Enel smart info device that will involve a 
representative sample of families served by the Carpinone primary sub-station. The scope of the project is to 
demonstrate whether giving to end users a feedback on their energy consumption can addres s more efficient

providers, research organisations and one large consumer, propose five large -scale demonstrations to show

Glanbia Ingredients Ireland Designated Activity Company  (GLAN) is a global nutrition company, grounded in

fresh ingredients including milk, whey and grains, and with its expert knowledge and capabilities produces high-
quality nutritional ingredients and branded consumer products for customers and consumers worldwide.  
 
GLAN employs over 6,000 people across 32 countries and its products are sold or distributed in over 130 countries 
with an annual turnover of €3.6 billion. GLAN’s major production facilities are located in Ireland, the US, the UK, 
Germany and China. It has three segments: Glanbia Performance Nutrition (number one global performance 
nutrition brand portfolio); Glanbia Nutritionals (focused on both dairy and non-dairy nutritional ingredients); and, 
Joint Ventures & Associates (whereby it has three strategic Joint Ventures and Associates: Southwest Cheese in 
the US, Glanbia Cheese in the UK and Glanbia Ireland). GLAN’s shares are listed on the Irish and London Stock 
Exchanges (symbol: GLB). 
Role in the project 
GLAN will participate in the Factories of the Future  field trials. UC1.1 will be based on GLAN’s maintenance 
function. Typically, key assets and equipment are being maintained using scheduled and usage-based maintenance 
strategies. Predictive maintenance uses key data feeds and agents to constantly monitor condition feeds and 
recognise patterns leading to equipment failure allowing for timely and effective intervention. The key benefit is 
that assets can be sweated for longer and avoid unplanned outages. GLAN will also participate in UC1.3, whereby

dedicating extensive resources to cognitive computing, as IBM leaders believe it will have a profound impact on

democratizing expertise, and transforming industries as well as professions. Last year, IBM announced that it has 
realigned its entire business strategy around cognitive computers, which can learn, reason, and efficiently process

4.1.13 INSTITUT FUR RUNDFUNKTECHNIK GMBH 
Short Name IRT 
 
Country Germany 
Type Small or Medium-size Enterprise 
Number of employees 134 
Website www.irt.de/en  
Short Profile 
Institut Fur Rundfunktechnik Gmbh (IRT) is an SME specialising in audio -visual media technologies. With 60 
years of experience, IRT is an internationally renowned research and competence centre for broadcast and media 
technology. IRT researches, observes and develops new technologies in the digital audiovisual media, always with 
the goal to strategically adjust the broadcast idea to new market environments and requirements. Founded in 1956, 
it is jointly owned by the Public Service Broadcasters of Germany, Austria and Switzerland (ARD, ZDF, DRadio, 
ORF and SRG/SSR). About 100 experienced engineers and researchers find innovative and real -world solutions 
which enhance the quality of radio, television and new media services. 
 
As a main motivation, IRT sees its role as that of a technical advisor to broadcasters, as well as a consulting body 
for industry. The institute collaborates internationally with numerous commercial companies, various research 
organisations and universities in the broadcasting, media, communications engineering and IT sectors.  
 
IRT is committed to preserving broadcasting in general, and public broadcasting in particular, in Europe and 
beyond. This commitment applies to new markets, upcoming technologies, emerging requirements and the move 
towards a data-driven economy in the media sector as well. IRT’s extensive experience enables it to provide its 
associates and other industry clients with reliable and knowledgeable services, by performing fundamental 
research, by developing new broadcasting/media technologies and by implementing feasible solutions for regular 
operation. To achieve its vision and to create open ecosystems also for 3rd party SMEs, IRT strongly favours open 
technical standards, interoperable APIs and horizontal system markets. Consequently, IRT is an active contributor 
to the relevant standardisation bodies and initiatives, including HbbTV which was co-founded by IRT, as well as 
ETSI, ITU and W3C. IRT is firmly involved in the technical work of the EBU (European Broadcasting Unio n) 
and is founding member of the European Technology Platform NEM (New European Media). IRT has substantial 
experience with national and international collaborative projects including H2020. 
 
Role in the project 
IRT’s primary role in 5G-SOLUTIONS will be to validate 5G infrastructures in the context of mass audio-visual 
media distribution by also extending IRT’s test facilities to align with the evolving 5G standards. Moreover, IRT, 
will provide and further evolve the QoE solution to enable systematic validation of 5G infrastructures for unicast 
content distribution. 
 
IRT will lead ‘T8.3 Standardisation’ using standardisation as a means to exploit the impacts of the project result 
and to most efficiently invest the public funding of this project. IRT will ensure that the research results produced 
by the project will be aligned with existing and emerging standards from the relevant standardisation bodies (e.g. 
3GPP, ETSI, ITU, IEEE, IETF, etc).

Relevant Projects 
1. 5G-Xcast [5G-PPP Phase 2]: ‘Broadcast and Multicast Communication Enablers for the Fifth-Generation of 
Wireless Systems’. The project will devise, assess and demonstrate large scale immersive media delivery by 
means of conceptually novel wireless technologies, contributing to the fur ther definition of 5G and its 
standardisation. 5G-Xcast will focus on large scale media distribution, as this use case is one of the most 
demanding requirements in terms of data rate (capacity), scalability (cost -effectiveness) and ubiquity 
(coverage). (01/06/2017 – 31/05/2019) http://5g-xcast.eu/. 
2. 5G-MEDIA [5G-PPP Phase 2]: ‘Programmable edge-to-cloud virtualization fabric for the 5G Media industry’ 
is a running project that aims at innovating media-related applications by investigating how these applications 
and underlying 5G networks should be coupled and interwork to the benefit of both: to ensure the applications 
allocate the resources they need to deliver high quality of experience and so that the network is not 
overwhelmed by media traffic. (01/06/2017 – 30/11/2019). http://www.5gmedia.eu/ 
3. 5G TODAY [Other]: coordinated by IRT, a running project to investigate and implement the 3GPP Rel.14 
specification for large-scale distribution of media content in a broadcast mode based on mobile technology.

4.1.14 IREN SPA 
Short Name IREN

Short Profile 
IREN SPA (IREN), is one of the largest and most dynamic multi-utility companies in Italy with its main corporate 
offices in Reggio Emilia and its operating units in Genoa, Turin, Parma, Piacenza, Reggio Emilia, La Spezia and 
Vercelli. IREN  operates in the sectors of electricity (production, distribution and sale), thermal energy for district 
heating (production and sale), gas (regasification, distribution and sal e), the management of integrated water 
services, environmental services (collection and disposal of waste) and energy services. 
 
The Group serves a multiregional catchment area, has 6 .420 employees, a portfolio of around 1.7 million 
customers in the energy sector and about 2.6 million inhabitants served in the integrated water and 2 million in the 
waste cycles. It is the first operator in Italy in the district heating sector for the volume heated, third in the water 
services sector for the number of cubic metres managed and in the environmental services sector for the quantity 
of waste treated, fifth in the gas sector for the amount of gas sold to end customers and fifth in the electricity sector 
for the amount of electricity sold.  Moreover, IREN is an eco-friendly electricity producer for more than 85% of 
its production. 
 
Iren is structured as an industrial parent company with separate companies in charge of the individual business 
lines. IREN handles the strategic development, coordination and monitoring of activities, while the four subsidiary 
operating companies ensure the coordination and development of the business lines: 
− Iren Energia in the electricity and heat energy production sector and the technological services sector; 
− Iren Mercato as regards the sale of electricity, gas and district heating; 
− IRETI in the gas and electricity distribution business and in the integrated water service; 
Iren Ambiente in the waste collection, in the design and management of wast e treatment and disposal 
plants and in the renewable energies sector. 
 
IREN’s work will be partly implemented by IREN Energia, IREN Mercato, and IREN Rinnovabili, subsidiaries of 
IREN, which will be considered as linked third parties within the framework of 5G-SOLUTIONS. Further details 
are provided at Section 4.2 Third parties involved in the project (including use of third-party resources) at Section 
4.2. 
Role in the project 
IREN mainly participates in the Smart Energy Living Lab. In particular, IREN will be responsible for the design, 
development and deployment of technical solutions needed for the execution of UC2.1  ‘Industrial Demand Side 
Management’ and UC2.2 ‘Electrical Vehicle Smart Charging’ in the test site of Torino. IREN will also participate 
in the testing activities for validation of the technical solution and performance evaluation.

Relevant Projects 
1. NeMo [EU]: ‘Hyper-Network for electroMobility ’. Electromobility is a major factor towards transport 
decarbonisation. However a number of challenges (limited charging options, lack of interoperability, absence 
of a unified identification/payment process, energy grid overload, expensive charging tariffs) limit the 
potential for interoperable and seamless electromobility services to a wider of actors and geographic area, 
hindering electromobility adoption. NeMo addresses all issues through a pan -European eRoaming Hyper -
Network that allows seamless and interoperable use of electromobility services throughout Europe. In addition 
it provides an Open Cloud Marketplace, where third parties can provide services (B2B2C) aiming to increase 
EV attractiveness. (01/10/2016 – 30/09/2019).  
2. FLEXMETER [EU]: ‘Flexible smart metering for multiple energy vectors with active prosumers ’ 
demonstration of a flexible smart metering architecture, based on cheap and already available components, 
that can be implemented in a plug and play way, combining metering of different services (electricity, water, 
gas, district heating), providing advanced services to  the users, to the DSOs and to the other utilities, and 
enhancing the possibilities of the retail market. (01/01/2015 – 31/12/2017). http://flexmeter.polito.it/.  
3. PLANET [EU]: ‘Planning and operational tools for optimising energy flows and synergies between energy 
networks’ aims to develop and provide a Decision Support System (PLANET DSS) to policy makers and 
network operators to help them facilitate the full integration of increasing intermittent renewable energy in the 
electricity grid. This will be possible through the global coordination of all energy (electricity, gas, heat) 
networks and assets, with special focus on energy storage and conversion techniques and assets. (01/11/2017 
– 31/10/2020).  
4. PUMP-HEAT [EU]: ‘Performance Untapped Modulation for Power and Heat via Energy Accumulation 
Technologies’ project aim is to develop and demonstrate up to TRL 6 in the relevant environment (a real 
Combined Cycle Cogenerative plant) an innovative, easily scalable, economically viable and replicable plant 
layout based on the integration of heat pumps (HP) and thermal energy storage, to un -tap Combined Cycle 
(CC) potential flexibility through low-CAPEX balance of plant innovations. The new Pump-Heat Combined 
Cycle (PHCC) will unlock the current situation of low operating-hours or mothballed (=temporarily suspended 
to operate) CC and Gas Turbine (GT) power plants. In fact, PUMP -HEAT will improve CCs flexibility and 
global efficiency, in order to strengthen their role in balancing fluctuations of electrical market with a high 
penetration of renewable sources (RES), while mitigating the effects of cyclic operation and service life 
expenditure, and reducing CO2 and pollutant emissions in these critical operating peri ods. (01/09/2017 – 
31/08/2020).  
Significant Infrastructure

The plants managed in Turin are composed of: 
− 10 HV/MV transformation stations; 
− 1,224 MVA HV/MV power transformation;

4.1.15 IRIS TECHNOLOGY SOLUTIONS, SOCIEDAD LIMITADA  
Short Name IRIS 
 
Country Spain

Short Profile 
IRIS Technology Solutions, Sociedad Limitada (IRIS) is a technology SME established in Barcelona in 2007 
specialising in the manufacture and integration of a Process Analytical Technology (PAT) based in real -time 
quality monitoring solutions for the process industries and IoT systems for smart manufacturin g, predominantly 
targeted at the food, pharmaceutical and chemical industries. In particular, the product line comprises proprietary 
state-of-the-art IR analysers for at -line and in -line process monitoring. On the one hand, IRIS offers solutions 
based on the latest developments in photonics-in the fields of MEMs Near Infrared Spectroscopy, Hyperspectral 
Imaging, and Raman.  On the other hand, the company leverages ICTs, whereby it applies Machine learning, 
Artificial Intelligence and Data Mining techniques for predictive and active control, as well as for decision support 
systems. In addition to photonics-based analysers, IRIS also works with IoT sensors for enabling equipment and 
machinery for smart manufacturing and transitioning industry to the Industry4.0 paradigm also providing solutions 
such as cloud-based for mobility, remote monitoring and multi-site applications. IRIS is ISO 9001:2008 certified 
and one of the few Spanish companies having UNE-EN-ISO 166002: Management Systems R&D&I certification. 
IRIS is also certified by the local (Catalonian) government as a provider of technological R&D services (Tecnio 
Certification).  
IRIS has a great experience in working in collaborative R&D projects in H2020, both as a coordinator and a partner 
in the SPIRE, FoF , and BBI programmes. As a photonics and ICT -based solutions provider for the process 
industries, IRIS’ business is very much relevant to stakeholders, in that the future deployment of 5G will accelerate 
the Industry 4.0 revolution; whereby fundamental to Industry 4.0 is the implementation of a reliable 
communication layer capable of dealing with an increase in several orders of magnitude the number of assets, 
volume, and variety of information and reaction times in future manufacturing systems. As such, IRIS’ leadership 
of the Factories of the Future vertical LL in 5G-SOLUTIONS is a strategic decision having the capacity to perform

well by understanding the industrial processing environments, and the development, manufacturing and integration

Role in the project 
IRIS will be responsible for the f acilitation in the living lab case studies in terms of organisation, planning, and

supercomputing will allow using updated machine learning algorithms for improving the current capabilities –
mainly based on rather simple chemometric tools. It ultimately implies more comprehensive (accurate) 
identification and quantification to take artificial vision to a wider paradigm: chemical vision.

4.1.16 LIVEU LTD 
Short Name LIVEU 
 
Country Israel  
Type Small or Medium-size Enterprise 
Number of employees ~100 
Website www.liveu.tv  
Short Profile 
LiveU Ltd (LIVEU) is a private company established in 2006 in Israel. It fully owns LiveU Inc., a USA subsidiary. 
LIVEU employs about 100 people, mostly engineers but also sales and customers support staff. It maintains offices 
in several countries, includ ing: Germany, UK, France, Russia, India, China and Hong Kong. LIVEU sets the 
standards for high -quality and reliable live video acquisition, management and distribution over IP. LIVEU’s 
award-winning technology enables live video transmission from any location around the world with lightweight, 
easy-to-use equipment. With top -tier customers in more than 70 countries, LIVEU’s solutions are being utilised 
to cover breaking and developing news and high -profile events, such as the FIFA World Cup™, Winter and 
Summer Olympic Games, Presidential Campaigns, Super Bowls, US Collegiate Championships and red -carpet 
events. Public safety and other government agencies have also been using LiveU bonding solutions. The solutions 
are being used from moving vehicles, trains,  undergrounds, drones, helicopters and near -shore ships, providing 
reliable high bandwidth bonded links for video uplink and bi-directional data delivery. LIVEU’s solutions include 
multiple 4G LTE/3G, HSPA cellular links, which are optimised for maximum video quality based on the available 
network conditions. L IVEU solutions can also bond WiFi, satellite links and fixed IP links. LIVEU has issued 
several core patents on bonding live video wireless transmission in the EU (validated in 14 European countries),  
Israel, USA and many more. The bonding products are basically SW and algorithms that take -in an audio/video 
feed from a camera, encode it, split the packets over the multiple connections available to it considering the 
momentary performance in each one of  them, to a remote IP at the customer premises or in the cloud where a 
LIVEU SW resides and reassemble the received packets into a comprehensible video stream output. Other 
products and technologies allow the delivery of live video over the public Internet , using standard ISPs, with no 
video quality loss and very minimal latency added. These are used to share live quality video between multiple 
sites and between agencies and affiliates. LIVEU core competencies are in video and data delivery, wireless 
networks including cellular, WiFi and satellite (SATCOM), using multiple connections bonded together for the 
video delivery. LIVEU’s expertise, achievements and reputation strongly correlate with the project’s overall vision 
and tasks and with the specific tasks  that LIVEU leads in it. LIVEU’s core ability to create a quality reliable 
broadband connection is a prime goal of the 5G KPIs. It is reflected in several verticals that the project intends to 
serve namely Media & Entertainment. 
Role in the project 
Deliver platforms for a mobile, reliable broadband over multiple relevant wireless links (multiple 5G connections, 
802.11p DSRC, satellite) for data and for professional grade video uplink.  These two platforms shall be used to 
demonstrate KPIs as well as for other partners to run their applications, using these links to communicate between 
the entities. 
 
LIVEU will lead WP6 ‘Enhanced User Experience field trials’, aiming to conduct advanced field trials in the 
vertical sectors of Media and Entertainment to validate the technological and business performance of 5G.  
Furthermore, as WP6 Leader, LIVEU will oversee all the undertaken efforts t o use the test results and data, in 
order to deliver impact analysis and impact assessment reports to sys tematically address the LL stakeholder 
perspectives. As a result, LIVEU will lead the following tasks: 
• T6.1 LL planning, setup and operational management 
• T6.2 LL4 execution: Media & Entertainment

Short Profile 
Ericsson is a world-leading provider of telecommunications equipment and services to mobile and fixed network 
operators. Over 1.000 networks in more than 180 countries use their network equipment, and more than 40 percent 
of the world’s mobile traffic passes through Ericsson networks. Ericsson offers end-to-end solutions for all major 
mobile communication standards and the networks, telecom services and multimedia solutions make it easier for 
people, across the world, to communicate.  
 
L.M. Ericsson Limited  (LMI) is playing a key role using innovation to empower people, business and society, 
working towards a Networked Society, in which everyone and everything can benefit from a connection they have. 
The company is a strong leader in 5G.  Ericsson’s Network M anagement Lab in Ireland carrying out applied 
research, developing new and innovative strategic solutions and technologies for service and telecommunication 
management in existing and emerging networks. The Lab is involved in bringing new ideas and competence into 
Ericsson, with a focus on Ericsson’s network management products, including areas of research such as: Predictive 
Analytics, Service Assurance, Big Data Visualisation, Recommendation Systems, etc. utilising Machine Learning, 
Data & Stream Mining, Complex Event Processing, Recommender Systems and Advanced Visualisation, and 
Cloud technologies. LMI has over 150 publications in conferences, workshops, journals, books and patents, and 
have also been involved for more than 10 years in EU projects, such as Marie Curie Actions - supported Distorm, 
Eureka Celtic Madeira, Eureka Celtic Magneto, FP7 PRISTINE, H2020 ARCFIRE. Additionally, LMI is actively

Short Profile 
NTNU, the Norwegian University of Science and Technology, aims at creating knowledge for a better world and 
solutions that can change everyday life. NTNU is a university with an international focus, with headquarters in 
Trondheim and campuses in Ålesund and Gjøvik. NTNU has a main profile in science and technology, a variety 
of programmes of professional study, and great academic breadth that also includes the humanities, social sciences, 
economics, medicine, health sciences, educational science, architecture, entrepreneurship, art disciplines and 
artistic activities. NTNU has eight faculties, the University Museum and University Library, more than 40 0 00 
students and 7 ,100 full -time equivalent employees. NTNU is committed to innovative education, especially 
increased use of learning methods with active student involvement and digitization. NTNU has four strategic areas 
of research in 2014–2023: sustainability, energy, oceans, and health. The university is also the host or partner for 
35 large research centres. Some nine per cent of NTNU’s students are international and NTNU has a wide 
international network. NTNU has offices in Japan and Brussels (togethe r with the University of Bergen and 
SINTEF).   
 
The Department of Mechanical and Industrial Engineering (MTP)  is one of eight departments at the Faculty of 
Engineering Science. MTP has broad interdisciplinary expertise in the fields of logistics, machine design, product 
development, materials science and risk and reliability of complex systems. The research at the department focuses 
on development, optimisation and improvement of industrial processes and production systems. One of MTP’s 
goals is to secure t he Norwegian industry and administration with access to knowledge and expertise on an 
international level. 
 
NTNU main tasks revolve around industrial use cases for 5G communication. NTNU can provide systems at an 
industrial scale, descriptions of these, architectures and requirement specifications for these test facilities for live 
demonstrations with moving and stationary robots using closed -loop control over 5G infrastructure while in 
presence of industrial operations such as arc welding while intensive c ommunication between remote operation 
equipment and operators takes place concurrently. 
 
The Robotics/Industry 4.0 laboratories have 12 industrial robots from Kuka and Universal Robotics as well as 2

Short Profile 
NUROGAMES GmbH (NURO) is an independent games development company, founded in early 2006  by 
practised experts of the games and media industry. Headquartered in Cologne Germany the company maintains 
representative offices in Barcelona and Berlin. Since April 2011, the Berlin -based lbxgames GmbH and lieblinx 
GmbH are a part of the company and form a strong strategic alliance.  
 
NURO covers a wide range of work experience, comprising high-skill development for mobile and cross-platform 
games, leisure applications being one of its main fields of activity. Another focus of the company is placed on the 
development of games for Xbox one (Kinect), Playstation 4, Playstation Vita, Nintendo 3DS, Nintendo DS and 
Nintendo Wii, Virtual Reality and Augmented Reality. Furthermore, NURO develops mobile games / applications 
and social games.  
 
The mobile division is specialising in the development, production and marketing of mobile applications for iOS 
and Android Smartphone and Tablet as well as contents, ranging from innovative applications like games, active 
screens, instant messaging etc. to pod-cast solutions. Currently, developments have been ordered for iPhone/iPad 
touch platforms and Android applications as application for other application stores as well (Windows 
Marketplace, Mac App Store, etc.). Further working fields include the development of web-based e-learning games 
and game-based e-learning evolutions as well as the realisation of online and browser games for an international 
market.  
 
By participating in multiple research projects on a national and international level, N URO ensures the long-term 
orientation and the knowledge of state -of-the art technologies. N URO’s team has many years of experience in 
research projects of the BMBF and the European Union. They include such projects as MaTHiSiS, PATHway. 
RAGE, 5GTANGO, SPIELBAR, MMOBG Development MEDIA.  
 
Role in the project 
In 5G -SOLUTIONS, NURO will contribute in the execution of  smart city use case s by providing relevant 
technology enablers (e.g. applications) and in particular leading the intelligent street lighting, smart parking and 
port safety use cases. NURO will also lead the market assessment and technology assessment in order to identify 
and verify that the use cases to be trialled are indeed the most relevant having the highest commercialisation 
interest and potential amongst the targeted vertical industries. NURO will coordinate and supervise the undertaking 
of the market survey assessment to understand the sectoral needs and opportunities for 5G-SOLUTIONS, with an 
initial focus on telecoms and SMEs.

3. PATHway [EU]: ‘ PATHway: Technology enabled behavioural change as a pathway towards better self -
management of CVD ’. PATHway proposes a radically novel approach to C ardiac Rehabilitation that will 
ensure a paradigm shift towards empowering patients to more effectively self -manage their Cardiovascular 
disease (CVD), set within a collaborative care context with health professionals. It has the potential to deliver 
significant cost savings t o the healthcare system, and direct more appropriate utilization of healthcare 
resources. This will be achieved via a patient -centric holistic approach that specifically addresses the above 
barriers. NURO creates an exergaming platform as well as an autono mous graphical avatar.  (01/02/2015 – 
30/09/2018). http://pathway2health.eu/.  
4. 5GTANGO [5G-PPP Phase 2]: ‘ 5G Development and validation platform for global industry -specific 
network services and Apps ’. 5GTANGO puts forth the flexible programmability of 5G networks with i) a 
NFV-enabled Service Development Kit (SDK), ii) a Store with advanced validation and verification 
mechanisms for VNFs/Network Services qualification (including 3rd party contributions) and iii) a m odular 
Service Platform in order to bridge the gap between business needs and network operational management 
systems. This end-to-end ecosystem for the agile development and deployment of services realises an extended 
NFV DevOps model between service devel opers, telecom operators and vertical industries, increasing 
operational efficiency, facilitating the implementation and validation of new services and accelerating the 
adoption of NFV technologies. 5GTANGO system is demonstrated in two vertical pilots: ad vanced 
Manufacturing and immersive Media. (01/06/2017 – 30/11/2019). https://5gtango.eu/.  
5. V4Design [EU]: ‘Visual and textual content re -purposing FOR (4) architecture, Design and video virtual 
reality games’. V4Design will develop a platform that provides architects, video game creators and designers 
of any expertise with innovative tools including VR tools necessary to enhance and simplify the creative phase 
of the designing process. The main idea behind V4Design is to reuse (i) visual: movies, documentaries 
paintings and images from other artwork and (ii) textual content: from textual documentations in films, critics, 
catalogues, museum guides, and re-purpose it in order in a way that will be useful for architecture and  video 
game designers. (01/01/2018 – 31/12/2020). https://v4design.eu/.

4.1.20 ORBIS MES 
Short Name OMES 
 
Country Ireland  
Type Small or Medium-size Enterprise 
Number of employees 20 
Website www.orbismes.com  
Short Profile 
Orbis MES Ltd. (OMES) is a software and systems integration company from Dublin, Ireland, established in 2011 
in order to provide Smart Manufacturing Execution Systems (MES) and Performance Management (SPM) 
Systems to the global food and beverage industry. The OPS™ Platform has been adopted by blue-chip customers 
including Diageo, Glanbia, Dean Foods and recently Dairy Farmers of America. Orbis OPS™ is a key solution 
for Manufacturing Operations and Performance Management (MOM/MI) and provides the data -hub to the 
enterprise, which is central to the evolution to Industrial Internet of Things (IIOT).  
 
In more detail, OPS™ provides manufacturers with the proven Operations and Performance Management 
functionality to effectively plan, schedule, execute, track, a nalyse, report and improve production processes. It 
also provides the plant with industrialised and robust platform for cross functional Performance Management from 
Realtime Plant Operations to Strategic and Global KPI’s. The Orbis OPS™ Solution for Smart Manufacturing 
provides process manufacturers with a powerful solution to Monitor Operations, to drive efficiencies and to 
produce sustainable, on-spec quality products. Furthermore, it enables the monitoring of performance from User 
Entry, Data Collection, Workflow, Data Analytics and Reporting to drive efficiencies according to a defined set 
of KPI’s.  
 
OMES are technological stakeholders in the Smart Manufacturing Space. They seek to be at the forefront of 
developments relating to 5G in order to enable their customers to harness the efficiencies and power of 5G through 
connected devices, services and collaborating functions across multiple sites. OMES believes that it can 
demonstrate 5G technology in action to its industrial partners Glanbia (GLAN), and va lidate the key 5G-PPP 
Network KPIs through the testing of multiple business scenarios within the Glanbia plant. Validating 5G 
technology in the Glanbia plant will reveal the efficiency they can gain through the adoption of 5G technology, 
especially for time-critical and not-time critical optimisation and communication within the digital factory.  
 
OMES is keen to facilitate this validation to demonstrate the power of 5G not only to the participant company, but 
also to its’ wider customer base. This validation will enable OMES to become a proponent of early 5G adoption, 
thus driving Factories of the Future within Europe. 
Role in the project 
OMES will be mainly involved in the Factories of the Future filed trials, and in particular in UC 1.1 and UC 1.2. 
In UC1.1, OMES with its client GLAN will enhance the operation of their Smart Manufacturing Execution 
Systems & Performance Management Systems, whereby the OPS Smart Manufacturing datahub – a centralised 
Hub for connectivity & data storage (for data input and extraction from various devices across the plant) – will be 
used for 5G validation to ensure efficiency, speed, capacity, latency, reliability, accuracy and timeliness in data 
input. In UC1.3, OMES will develop an AR module of a  GLAN powder plant to validate key KPIs through the 
testing of multiple business scenarios within the plant.

Short Profile 
The University of Patras (UoP) is the third largest university in Greece with each own campus in the outskirts of 
Patras city. The University of Patras includes 24 Departments, with a large number of sectors and consequently a 
great range of disciplines, which operate 161 laboratories and 17 fully equipped clinics.  UoP has 32,398 
Undergraduate and 3,781 Postgraduate students, a total of 633 faculty members, 191 Teaching and Technical staff 
and 357 Administrative Personnel. Besides its distinguished path in education, the UoP has excelled in the fields 
of Basic and Applied Research. The UoP has acquired international prominence for pioneering wide ranging 
Research in areas such as Environment, Health, Biotechnology, Mechanics, Electronics, Informatics and Basic 
Science. A number of the Departments, Laboratories and Clinics have been designated as Centres of Excellence, 
This proposal version was submitted by Frini LAZAROU on 14/11/2018 13:54:55 Brussels Local Time. Issued by the Participant Portal Submission Service.
 
G                                                                                                                                                   Page 154 
 
on the basis of International Assessment. The university has a reputation for quality and innovative research and 
presents an effective participation in a plethora of Research Projects, Scientific Organi sations, and Research 
Groups. 
 
The Network and Management Architecture Group (NAM), established in 2005, belongs to the Division of 
Telecommunications & Information Technology. NAM group has built its expertise in a number of scientific and 
technology areas as a result of international and national collaborations with industry and research projects, 
primarily European. The research activities of the group revolve around networking technologies and networked 
services and t heir application to various application domains. NAM group is currently carrying ou t important 
research in a number of key areas for the next generation internet, 5G/SDN/NFV H2020 Projects: 5G-VINNI [5G-
PPP Phase 3]: The 5G Verticals Innovation Infrastructure initiative. 
 
The Network Architectures and Management (NAM) group which represent the research aspect of the Greek 
cluster in this project acquired its expertise through collaborations with industry and a series of research national 
and European projec ts. It is currently comprised of two professors, four post-docs, two researchers-system 
developers and seven PhD students. During the last ten years , UoP has been involved in many Future Internet 
Research (FIRE) projects: Panlab-PII, OpenLab, FORGE and coordinated others like VITAL++ and STEER. We 
are also the technical leaders of 5GinFIRE project, which targets to enable experimentation on top of 5G resources 
and infrastructures. We are also maintainers of http://sence.city a service that engages citizens to report issues 
across their city and the ThingsNetwork IoT infrastructure/community in Patras. Finally, UoP has participated and 
successfully completed Proof of Concept #14 for the NFV ISG and performed two successful demonstrations in 
IETF’s 88 and 90. 
Role in the project 
UOP as part of the 5G -VINNI project, will implement one of the four 5G -VINNI facilities in the area of city of 
Patras in the Western Region of Greece . In this context,  UOP will host and provide operational support for 
multimedia use cases. It will also interconnect and interoperate with the 5G-VINNI Norway ICT-17 facility that 
will also host service components of similar use cases in order to support cross-domain communication scenarios 
and service deployments of verticals. In addition, UOP will provide and install: 
• Two new 5G RAN nodes which will act as 5G private networks to validate the stringent URLLC UC 
requirements within two factory locations, one in Ireland (GLAN) and the other in Brussels (PGBS); 
▪ One new 5G RAN node in IBM’s campus premises in Dublin-Ireland, whose traffic will be backhauled to 5G-
VINNI Patra ICT-17 facility.  
All RAN and core equipment provided by UOP will incrementally be upgraded to the latest 3GPP releases to allow 
the iterative testing and validation of the use cases to the latest available releases.

Relevant Projects 
1. 5G-VINNI [5G-PPP Phase 3]: ‘5G Verticals Innovation Platform’ will accelerate the uptake of 5G in Europe 
by providing an end-to-end (E2E) facility that validates the performance of new 5G technologies by operating 
trials of advanced vertical sector services. The 5G-VINNI strategy to achieve this involves: (1) Designing the 
most advanced 5G facility to demonstrate that technical and business 5G KPIs can be met, (2) Building and 
operating 7 interworking instances of the E2E facility to prove the capabilities and openness of the system, (3) 
Creating user friendly zero -touch orchestration, operations and management systems for the 5G -VINNI 
facilities to ensure operational efficiencies and optimal resource use, (4) Proving the 5G -VINNI capabilities 
through extensive experiments and measurements of performance against the 5G  KPIs, (5) Developing a 
viable 5G ecosystem model to support the NaaS infrastructure provision as a sustainable business beyond the 
project, and (6) Promoting the value of 5G -VINNI results to the relevant standards bodies and open source 
communities. The 5 GVINNI E2E facility will demonstrate the achievement of 5G KPIs across a range of 
combinations and permutations of new 5G access technologies and end-user equipment types interconnected 
by the most advanced 5G core network technologies available. The 5G -VINNI facilities include seven 
infrastructure instances in nationally supported 5G nodes across Europe; this number may be expanded as the 
ICT-19 projects come on-line in 2019. (started 01/07/2018) https://www.5g-vinni.eu/.  
2. 5GinFIRE [EU]: 5GinFIRE objective is to build and operate an Open, and Extensible 5G NFV -based 
Reference (Open5G -NFV) ecosystem of Experimental Facilities that not only integrates existing FIRE 
facilities with new vertical-specific ones but also lays down the foundations for instantiating fully softwarised 
architectures of vertical industries and experimenting with them.  (01/01/2017 – 31/12/2019). 
https://5ginfire.eu/  
Significant Infrastructure

− The BSS/OSS experimentation portal;

Short Profile 
Procter & Gamble Services Company NV (PGBS) is a global leader in consumer products with thousands of 
innovators in development centres and more than 20 plants. The PGBS’ Innovation Centre (BIC) performs key 
activities for holistic product innovation for Fabric and Home Care products. These activities include technology 
development, consumer understanding, product, package and process design, industrial and brand design as well

as engineering. It is one of the 3 Mega Innovation Hubs in Europe. These mega -hubs contain all the elements 
necessary to invest in the innovation of both existing and new products. PGBS’ BIC hosts over 50 nationalities, 
which provides researchers and students a unique chance to experience living in a multicultural environment. The 
BIC site has a yearly investment in >1000 people and more than 100 million euro in innovation for the fabric and 
home care products. It covers products like laundry detergents, dish products, fabric enhancers and air care 
products. It contains all the requirements for generating innovation, from idea generation to pilot plants and lead-
lines. The engineers and digitisation experts develop the strategies and approaches for the collaboration and 
deployment across the plants in Europe. Technology avenues such as big data analysis of plant data and process 
analytics are created in the Brussels Innovation centres and then implemented in the plants in Europe. This is 
enabled by a collaboration between process R&D experts, process engineers and chemists. The product of soluble 
unit dose is the most complex up to date as it combines both the processing of complex liquid chemical mixtures 
and assembly of mechanical components. BIC has a pilot facility and a lead-line for these products. In addition, it 
leads the engineering for implementation with the production plants in Mechelen and Amiens. 
 
Role in the project 
PBGS will participate as an industrial end-user in the Factories of the Future use cases. In particular, in UC1.1, to 
enable full automation of a digital plant, leveraging advanced technology, such as visual recognition of quality 
control on, for instance, bottles on a line, and hyperspectral imaging of co mplex products and vision systems on 
advanced robotics. The data needs to be collected and optimised across plants; In UC1.2, for tracking of materials 
(e.g. spare parts) and tracking of product stocks; In UC1.3 related to next generation plant planning/scheduling to 
increase plant productivity by better utilisation of the assets, 5G will enable  PBGS to bring this to the next level 
across sites and with new algorithms for dynamic, reactive scheduling; In UC1.4 home services will be validated 
for laundry that require connected machines t o continuously track and anticipate consumer laundry (imaging & 
spectral data).

Short Profile 
The Promozione per l Innovazione fra Industria e Universita Associazione (PIIU) is a not-for-profit organisation 
specialising in Innovation Management with the aim to promote technological innovation as well as impro ve 
transfer of know-how between industries, with a focus on SMEs, and Research Centres.  
 
Its Members are ICT experts and professionals working in the world of technological innovation in various 
industrial project settings. The focus of the Association is to identify the contexts, forms and methods to drive 
efficiently the communication, col laboration and linkage among industries, recogni sing that effective 
collaboration is key to the mutual ability to innovate and improve the occurrence of Innovation Based Technology. 
At a national level, PIIU is collaborating with over 100 industrial partners in many multidisciplinary projects. At 
an international level, there is strong involvement in European collaborative R&D projects, especially in the Future 
Internet and Big Data areas. 
Role in the project 
PIIU will contribute in the creation and maintenance of the concrete plan for the dissemination and use of 
knowledge of the project. Moreover, PIIU will participate in the dissemination actions of the project in scientific 
and business events and will be responsible for the project’s visibility through online channels, such as the online 
social media channels. PIIU will also participate in the activities related to the involvement of external SMEs with 
a specific program in order to accelerate the European ICT ecosystem by creating and supporting new businesses 
by unlocking the commercial potential of high -value solutions offered by 5G SOLUTIONS in line with the 
stakeholders’ engagement and community building strategy. PIIU will lead T9.3 Community Building (EAB setup, 
participation in 5G-PPP WGs, SB, TB).

changing regulatory regimes, the competitive environment and new technology platforms driving changes in the

Short Profile 
Waterford Institute of Technology (WIT) is the major provider of higher education in the South East region of 
Ireland and one of the largest Institutes of Technology's in Ireland. The Institute's range and scope reflect the 
changing needs of the southeast as well as the country’s as a whole. WIT hosts the Telecommunications Software 
& Systems Group (TSSG). TSSG is an internationally recognized centre of excellence for ICT research and 
innovation. It carries out a wide spectrum of industry -informed research in Information and Communications 
Technologies (ICT), particularly techn ologies enabling communications and information services. TSSG’s four 
key prioritised technical research areas include: Mobile Platforms and Services, Security Privacy and Identity, 
Data Analytics and Social computing and finally, Adaptive Networks and services. TSSG creates economic impact 
by translating its knowledge base and innovation into leading edge products and services by continuing their 
engagement with Industry in collaborative R&D, knowledge generation and transfer. Over the past five years, 
TSSG has delivered innovative solutions to over 110 Irish companies, and has created 11 spin -out companies in 
the South East including the award winning FeedHenry, a ground-breaking mobile cloud platform company, and 
ZolkC, a leading provider of mobile technology for international visitor attractions. The TSSG maintains an active 
group in the Intelligent transport system (ITS) with specific focused areas of interest as follows: 
− 5G: Automotive / Transport Vertical. 
− V to X communications. 
− Smart Urban Transport/ Context-Aware Platforms. 
− Mobility as A Service 
 
TSSG is also merging its decades of experience delivering successful ICT research, with the needs and expertise 
of the Life Sciences and Healthcare sectors. They have successfully built partnerships with both  academia and 
industry to progress the digital health research field and deliver end solutions to their industry partners. The Future 
Health Lab is committed to achieving better health outcomes through their focus on the following thematic areas: 
− Pervasive Sensing & IoT. 
− Gait and Movement Analysis. 
− Molecular Communications & Synthetic Biology. 
− Clinical Data as a Service (CDaaS). 
− VR Neurorehabilitation/Adaptation. 
− mHealth Technologies

results of this work in the management of 5G networks in the 5G -SOLUTIONS project. WIT will lead T1.4 
Methodology for the definition of test reports format, parameters and test points, and benchmarking for the results. 
WIT is expected to reinforce their  understanding of 5G network in different verticals and further consolidate 
expertise in 5G, ITS and relevant areas. The research work of 5G will be carried out in both the application level 
and the theoretical study level, to validate core 5G slicing, virtualisation technologies, architectures and 
corresponding KPIs linked to specific use cases and scenarios within 5G-SOLUTIONS.

mobility in Future internet, federated testbed management and Embedded software quality assurance and testing. 
Frances has multiple years of experience as a EU Project coordinator of SecCord and Effectsplus EU FP7 CSA 
funded research projects that relates to trust and security (responsible for security research project clustering, 
leading to increased collaboration, dissemina tion, networking strategic research agenda’s, road mapping and 
research to industry translation. Frances has also successfully Project coordinated and actively lead the 
Cybersecurity & Privacy (CSP) Forum initiative funded via the EU FP7 SecCord project, this project focused on 
EU research collaboration, networking  and clustering activities of funded EU trust and security research projects. 
With 12 years’ experience of working in EU funded research projects, Frances also over the past 2 years has

mobility, transport and automotive related research thematic areas (e.g. ADAS, MaaS, intelligent/Smart transport 
and mobility and the adoption and use of I CT technologies to intelligent transport systems, physical Internet).

Significant Infrastructure 
The National Cloud Networking testbed 
WIT/TSSG operate the National Cloud Networking testbed which is used by Irish and European SMEs and 
research institutes to develop products in controlled environments. The WIT/TSSG also offer consultancy services 
on the planning and deve lopment of data analytics solutions over a broad range of disciplines, including 
Agriculture, Telecommunications, Social Networking and Health. 
This proposal version was submitted by Frini LAZAROU on 14/11/2018 13:54:55 Brussels Local Time. Issued by the Participant Portal Submission Service.
 
G                                                                                                                                                   Page 165 
 
 
The TSSG SDN Testbed consists of physical and virtual SDN equipment as well as a pan -Ireland 4-node SDN 
live deployment built at the optical level and using 10GE as its switching layer. This lets researchers build and test 
new protocols that make large networks work in isolation but with the confidence of working outside of a 
simulation.  
The WIT/TSSG has its own High-Density Water Cooled Data Centre with an Electrical capacity of 300kVA. 
Existing services/ infrastructure available from the Data Centre include: 
• A 40-node OpenStack compute Cloud; 
• A 100TB Hadoop Cluster; 
• A 4-node pan-Ireland 10GE SDN testbed; 
• A 4-node SDR.field deployment over 175 acres; 
• A 6-node physical SDN deployment; 
• A virtual SDN deployment (cloud-based). 
 
Communication equipment for V2X communication 
A V2X communication system (mainly based on the ITS-G5 in the access layer) will be demonstrated in our EU 
project TransSec. The equipment can be utilised to conduct a comparative study between an ITS-G5 based V2X 
communication solution and a 5G solution. In addition, a heterogeneous solution can be studied to combine the 
characters of ITS-G5 (802.11p based DSRC) and 5G (Cellular V2X) to enhance the overall experience of the 
V2X communication.

4.1.26 YARA INTERNATIONAL ASA 
Short Name YARA  
Country Norway 
Type Industrial 
Number of employees >16.000 
Website www.yara.com  
Short Profile 
Yara International Asa (YARA) is a world-leading fertilizer company and a supplier of environmental solutions 
located in Norway. YARA was founded in 1905 as a solution for the European famine that swept over the continent 
in the early part of the 20th century. Since then,  YARA is continuously developing solutions that improve and 
increase global food pro duction in a sustainable way. Through this expertise, we have also managed to create 
additional environmental solutions that reduce harmful emissions.  
Currently, the company has more than 16,000 employees  and as a truly international company with production, 
sales and services, research and support operations in the Americas, Europe, Africa and Asia.  Yara's knowledge, 
products and solutions grow farmers', distributors' and industrial customers' businesses profitably and responsibly, 
while protecting the ea rth's resources, food and environment. Its fertilizers, crop nutrition programs and 
technologies increase yields, improve product quality and reduce the environmental impact of agricultural 
practices. Its industrial and environmental solutions improve air quality by reducing emissions from industry and 
transportation, and serve as key ingredients in the production of a wide range of goods. YARA fosters a culture 
that promotes the safety of employees, contractors and societies. 
Role in the project 
In 5G-SOLUTIONS, YARA will demonstrate the capabilities of 5G technology to support real-time operation and 
integration support for autonomous assets in a logistics hub at Herøya, Porsgrunn. The smart port will be a hub 
where autonomous assets are received and served with logistics support. The test site will have a 4,5G smart port 
infrastructure in place by 2020, developed in the project Yara Birkeland, integrating a dedicated autonomous vessel 
(Birkeland) with autonomous land -based cargo handling assets. The  UC 3.5 will explore the enhanced service 
offering enabled by 5G technology. 
 
Operation of Herøya port’s autonomous infrastructure (cranes, carriers, energy infrastructure etc) to serve multiple 
(not pre-defined) assets with on - and offloading as well as fuelling/charging and potentially basic maintenance. 
Multi-access cloud applications with assured quality connectivity and handle the integration between the assets to 
provide optimised logistics operations. Safety and security are key priorities in the des ign of the system and will 
be given focus in the development. 
 
YARA will be mainly involved in the Smart Cities & Ports  field trials in an attempt to u nderstand how 5G 
technology can enable autonomous operations in Smart Port and enable the digital factory . In particular, YARA 
will validate in UC 3.5 an autonomous cargo vessel and autonomous land-based cargo logistics handling assets in 
real operations a t Herøya port  over the 5G VINNI Norway facility extended by Herøya 5G RAN node . This 
includes the smart port and logistics to the plant cargo loading area, which will be operated in a mixed traffic 
environment. 
Key Personnel 
Thor Oterholt (Male) hold an MSc in process automation. He has more than 22 years of experience in the design, 
implementation and management of projects related to process control and safety systems for plant and building 
automation. He started his career at Hydro Agri Porsgrunn in 1995 and is moving to the role of discipline lead for 
safety and automations systems at Yara HUB unit in Porsgrunn, after 17 years in the system integration / vendor 
area of the industry.  Experience include FEED, integration, typical development, im plementation, testing and 
staging of various systems. He has also been involved in proposal preparation as system architect and heading off 
technical qualification programs with major customers both at a national and international level. Thor has six years 
of experience in safety and automations systems and associated systems & communications in Chemical and 
Fertilizer industry, six years of experience in Pharmaceutical industry and ten years of experience in Oil & Gas 
industry. 
 
Arve Haavik (Male)  is a Senior System Engineer at YARA since 2015. He holds a MSc degree in Process 
Automation from University of South -Eastern Norway. Arve has worked with extensively with control systems 
and he is also responsible for the production network, some of the applications within this area, and IT Security.

Key Personnel Profiles 
 
Prof. Francesco Delli Priscoli (Male)  is a graduate of Electronic Engineering "summa cum laude" from the 
"Sapienza" University of Rome in 1986. He received the PhD. in system engineering from the "Sapienza" 
University of Rome in 1991. From 1986 to 1991 he worked in the "Studies and Experiment ation" Department of 
Telespazio (Rome). Since 1991 he is working at "Sapienza" University of Rome where, at present, he is Full 
Professor and holds the courses "Automatic Controls" and "Control of Communication and Energy Networks". In 
the framework of his activity, he has mainly researched on resource/service/content management procedures and 
on cognitive techniques for telecommunication and energy networks, by largely adopting control based 
methodologies. He is the author of about 180 papers appeared on major international reviews (about 65), on books 
(about 10) and conferences (about 120) and of five patents. He is an associate editor of Control Engineering 
Practice and a member of the IFAC Technical Committee on "Networked Systems". He was/is the scienti fic 
responsible, at the "Sapienza" University of Rome and CRAT, for more than 30 projects financed by the European 
Union (fourth, fifth, sixth, seventh and eighth framework programmes) or by the European Space Agency (ESA), 
as well as for many national pro jects and co -operations with major industries. His present research interests 
concern closed -loop multi -agent learning techniques for Quality of Experience (QoE) evaluation and QoE 
assurance in advanced communication and energy networks, as well as all related networking algorithms. 
 
Dr Alessandro Di Giorgio (Male) is a Physicist in the field of Electronics and Cybernetics. He received his PhD 
in System Engineering in 2010 at "Sapienza" University of Rome. Since 2007, he has been working at CRAT. 
Since 2011, he is an Assistant Professor in Automatic Control. His research activity deals with the application of 
control systems theory to Smartgrids, with specific focus on active demand, electric vehicles smart charging and 
real time control of power networks. He is author of about 50 scientific papers on major international journals and 
conference proceedings. He has worked in seven research projects founded in Italian and European FP7 and 
Horizon 2020 programs.

After careful consideration of the human and technical resources necessary to implement the action, ENEL deems 
necessary to activate subcontracts for the implementation of certain action tasks. More precisely, subcontracting 
is deemed necessary for providing support for analysis/post-processing of data coming from e-Mobility activities 
performed principally in Task 4.3 ‘LL2 Vertical: Energy’ so as to generate reliable inputs to correlated tasks in 
the same Work Package (Task 4.1 ‘LL planning, setup & operat ional management’ and Task 4.4 ‘Performance 
evaluation and lessons learned’) and eventually to other WPs, such as WP8, in which post-processed data will be 
relevant for developing sound business, marketing and sustainability plans. These cleansed and/or analyzed data 
may be employed too, directly or indirectly, in journals and white papers (Task 9.1 ‘Dissemination and 
communication activities’) published together with other partners.  
 
Subcontracting will cover only a limited part of the action as it will r elate to the following task in which ENEL 
participates: 
▪ Task 5.2: LL2 Smart Energy 
 
In these tasks, subcontracting will relate to data analysis service for post -processing of data from e -mobility 
activities in the Energy Living Lab, namely: 
▪ Data handling and cleansing; 
▪ Statistical analyses using suitable statistical methodologies to be shared with ENEL; 
▪ Describe data in terms of key elements relating to the use-case analyzed, for instance power-time curves. 
 
A subcontract will be signed for the above contribution with a single contractor.

Section 5: Ethics and Security
5.1 Ethics 
The 5G-SOLUTIONS project will support EU’s 5G policy by implementing the last phase of the 5G cPPP roadmap. 
It aims to prove in the field that the 5G capabilities provide ubiquitous access to a wide range of forward -looking 
applications and services with orders of magnitude of improvement over the  current technology and infrastructure, 
thus bringing the 5G vision closer to fulfilment. This will be achieved through conducting advanced field trials of 
innovative use cases, directly involving end-users across five most plausible industry vertical domains (Factories of 
the Future, Smart Energy, Smart Cities , Smart Ports and Media & Entertainment) over 5G end -to-end facilities 
leveraged from ICT-17. To do so, the 5G-SOLUTIONS consortium works directly with telecom operators, leading 
telecom vendors R&D, world leading ICT solution providers , vertical industry leaders acting as end -users, SMEs 
and renowned research organisations/academia. Consequently, in 5G-SOLUTIONS, ethics refer to the involvement 
of human beings in the research process on the one hand, and the processing of personal data throughout the project’s 
lifetime on the other one. 
 
Nevertheless, the 5G-SOLUTIONS project is specifically designed to identify, analyse and integrate a consideration 
of any legal, ethical or social issues raised by the project and solution, and to identify and implement elements which 
would foster trust, usability and social acceptance. In fact, the consideration of these issues, and the embedding of 
privacy- and ethics-by-design, is a key way in which 5G-SOLUTIONS represents progress beyond the start-of-the-
art. Given this, the 5G-SOLUTIONS consortium is committed to show appreciation of potential ethical issues that 
may arise during the course of the project and as such, it has defined a set of procedures on how  to deal with ethics 
in a responsible way. 
 
In addition, concerning risk management and legal compliance, all participants to the project have to be aware of 
their obligations as potential data processers (where appropriate) as well as issues beyond data and info rmation 
protection and privacy described above. Actions should be taken to ensure that those handling subjects identifiable 
or sensitive information are made fully aware of their responsibilities and obligations to respect confidentiality in 
compliance wit h market standards (e.g.: ISO/IEC 27001:2005), best practices and legal requirements under the 
GDPR. In addition to the more general and EU wide guidelines, partners will adhere to and respect national 
regulations and laws. All partners are aware of their responsibilities in that sense and will follow the established rules. 
 
5.1.1 Humans being involvement in the project’s research process  
For example, in relation to informed consent, the consortium will adhere to the following principles. All stakeholder 
engagement activities (pilots, trials, workshops, etc.) will be conducted using fully rational adults, which means that 
they will be in a position to understand their role in the project. Participan ts will be given information on who will 
benefit from their participation in the research and what risk or burden they are undertaking by participating. The 
consortium will also provide information about the potential for commercial exploitation of the res earch. 
Participation in these aspects of the 5G-SOLUTIONS project will be fully voluntary and all participants will be 
given the opportunity to ask questions and receive understandable answers before making decisions about their 
participation. Participants will also have the right to withdraw themselves and their personal data and terminate 
their participation in the research at any time  and will be reminded about their rights before participation. 
Participants will be given this information via an information sheet and be asked to sign a consent form to document 
and verify the information they have been given. During the research, informed consent forms will be used for pilot 
testing and workshops with experts. The 5G-SOLUTIONS Draft Information sheet and i nformed consent form are 
provided in the Optional Annex 3: Ethics supporting document(s). 
 
With specific relation to national ethical requirements, 5G-SOLUTIONS will undertake specific reviews of the 
research to be conducted.  
 
First, 5G-SOLUTIONS will be guided by the ethical codes of all the partners.  
 
Should the EC request national assessments in pilot countries (e.g. Ireland, Belgium, Italy, Greece, Norway)  in 
addition to these mechanisms, the project coordinator will liaise with the Project Officer to identify potential review 
mechanisms. All reviews will include a consideration of the objectives, methodology and potential impact of the 
This proposal version was submitted by Frini LAZAROU on 14/11/2018 13:54:55 Brussels Local Time. Issued by the Participant Portal Submission Service.
 
G                                                                                                                                                   Page 176 
 
activities undertaken in the 5G-SOLUTIONS project. This robust review cycle will ensure that the project complies 
with national and European legislation (including privacy and data protection legislation) and with the ethical 
principles associated with research with humans and R esponsible Research and Innovation principles. Task T10.5 
‘Legal and Ethics’ will ensure that project’s research activities and pilot testing are ethically sound and that data 
from research participants is processed according to EU and national regulations  to ensure their privacy. This work 
will culminate in the delivery of the Ethics Protocol for the 5G-SOLUTIONS project, which will be delivered after 
a careful assessment of potential ethical concerns relating to the project’s activities. The Protocol will  comprise of 
ethical evaluation and guidelines, an information sheet and informed consent form, and will outline the ethical 
guidelines to project partners and will present a careful ethical evaluation of the project methodology and its 
compliance with EU and national policy on research ethics and data protection.   
 
Where required, this task will also seek approval from relevant national authorities. However, as many review bodies 
are flooded with requests for review, these procedures will begin at the com mencement of the project, and initial 
guidelines will be provided in M4, with the production of the 5G-SOLUTIONS Ethics Protocol (as part of D10.4 
Report on legal and ethics monitoring), well before the final planning of the solution and the deployment in Living 
Labs (starting in M 13). Throughout the project, the implementation of the Ethics Protocol will be monitored and 
refined including an update on the review procedures.”  
 
5.1.2 Objectives, methodology and impact 
The 5G-SOLUTIONS project includes objectives related to legal, social and ethical analysis. The GDPR introduces 
many new legal requirements that service providers and other stakeholders need to be able to implement in a way 
which is not overly burdensome and provides appropriate user control over data. A consideration of all these issues 
occurs through the respect for responsible research and innovation, research ethics and legal social and ethical issues 
in the project’s objectives.  
 
In 5G-SOLUTIONS, this will occur through a specific consideration of legal, social and ethical issues in relation to 
the project methodology, objectives and impact, via Work package 10 ‘Project management’, and specifically T8.4 
Innovation, data management and IPR activities’ and T10.5 ‘Legal and Ethics’ which identify research ethics and 
data protection requirements respectively. Privacy, data security and societal requirements will also be explicated in 
Task 1.1 ‘Definition and detailed analysis of vertical use cases/scenarios, baseline and corresponding target KPIs’ 
to provide foundational support for examining these issues in the project.  
 
5.1.3 Personal data processing  
All personal data are subject to national and European data protection and security regula tions. 5G-SOLUTIONS 
will address the overall legal framework that is stated in the General Data Protection Regulation (Regulation 
2016/679) on the protection of natural persons with regard to the processing of personal data and on the free 
movement of such data and repealing Directive 95/46/EC (General Data Protection Regulation - GDPR). Also, it will 
consider the relevant procedures for protecting citizens’ rights as reported by EGE and as proclaimed in the Charter 
of Fundamental Rights of the European Union (2000/C 364/01). 
 
Data storage will be secured and access by unwanted third parties will be prevented. Appropriate procedures will be 
applied for data collection (and their usage) and the methodology that will be employed for collecting, using and 
storing various data and information.  
 
Security policies and access management controls will be used in the project using security technologies that will 
record and process timestamped data such as user and device IDs, IP addresses, accessed assets, length of connection, 
etc. Therefore, personal data could be collected during these activities.  
 
As a general rule, the personal data will be processed anonymously and in an aggregated way (personal data collected 
from 5G-SOLUTIONS will be treated as highly confidential, respecting p rivacy) with GDPR-compliancy in mind. 
However, in the eventuality of personal data processing , the subjects involved will provide informed consent, 
expressed in a formal agreement. 5G-SOLUTIONS will collect and process data that are strictly necessary for the 
research. All of the individuals participating in the pilot activities will be volunteers and will have the project data 
collection, storage and processing plans explained to them before the activity begins. Should they wish to exclude 
themselves from the activity, or should they wish their data to be anonymised after the activity, the consortium will 
This proposal version was submitted by Frini LAZAROU on 14/11/2018 13:54:55 Brussels Local Time. Issued by the Participant Portal Submission Service.
 
G                                                                                                                                                   Page 177 
 
oblige and write to them to confirm (a) that their wishes have been carried out and (b) precisely how their wishes 
have been carried out. 
 
Moreover, 5G-SOLUTIONS does not involve the processing of genetic information. 
 
Data protection legislation, standards and best practices will be applied on the data collection, storage, protection, 
retention and destruction. The related GDPR-compliant procedures for data collection, storage, protection, retention, 
destruction or re -use as well as data safety procedures will be developed as part of Task  T8.4 ‘Innovation, data 
management and IPR activities’. In addition, Task T10.5 Legal and Ethics led by Carmela Occhipinti (CEL) 5G-
SOLUTIONS’s Legal & Ethics Manager (L&EM) and Data Protection Officer (DPO), in collaboration with partners 
ethical committees and internal data privacy single point of contacts, will support project partners to adopt common 
procedures ensuring that 5G-SOLUTIONS research activities and pilot testing are ethically sound and that data from 
research participants is stored according to EU and national regulations to ensure their privacy. 
 
Most of the documentation associated with these ethi cal and legal reviews are not yet available, nor would it be 
appropriate to approach the relevant experts before the project is funded. However, the consortium is happy to provide 
the draft information sheets consent forms to be used by project in the Optional Annex 3 – Ethics supporting 
documents and will provide the remaining material by the deadlines agreed in the description of Work package 10 
‘Project management’ as part of Task 8.4 and Task 10.5 (deliverables D8.4 and D10.4). The documentation to be 
provided will include:  
▪ Feedback from ethical review activities; 
▪ Revised informed consent forms and project information sheets; 
▪ Any other relevant communications regarding ethical approvals
5.2 Security  
5G-SOLUTIONS will not involve:  
• Activities or results raising security issues;  
• 'EU-classified information' as background or results.  
 
This initial assessment does not preclude a different assessment following the security scrutiny. Should the members 
of the Information and C ommunication Technologies  Programme Committee  consider that 5G -SOLUTIONS 
involves security-related activities or produces outputs that need to be classified, special provisions for classified  
information (as defined in the Commission Rules of Procedure (Decision 2015/444/EC, ECSC, Euratom, and further 
explained in the Guidelines for the classification of research results) will be taken in the grant agreement, as necessary 
and appropriate.

Annex 3: Ethics Supporting Documents  
 
5G-SOLUTIONS Draft Information sheet and informed consent form 
Information Sheet           [Date] 
 
 
5G Solutions for European Citizens 
 
I consent to participate in the European Union-funded1 5G-SOLUTIONS research project coordinated by Telecom, 
Italia SPA, Italy in partnership with [Insert NAME of the INSTITUTION2]. I am aware that the purpose of this project 
is to conduct advanced field trials of thematically diverse digital services that require 5G capabilities in the vertical 
domains of Factories of the Future, Smart Energy, Smart Cities, Smart Ports and Media & Entertainment, directly 
engaging end-user actors, so as to validate the technological performance of 5G technology in successfully being 
able to serve them, as well as the business potential of such use cases prior to commercial deployment.  
The findings of this survey / interview / workshop / field trial / group discussion / other 
(Specify:………………………..)3 will assist the project partners  to assess and validate the technological and 
business performance of 5G through innovative use cases in the aforementioned domains. I understand that any 
personal data I provide will be handled according to the legal requi rements outlined in the General Data Protection 
Regulation (Directive 95/46/EC). 
I understand that I am participating in this research voluntarily and that I am free to leave at any time, without any 
impacts on me or my future participation in the project.  I am also aware that I am free to refuse to answer any 
questions or provide any information that I do not wish to discuss. I understand that I have the right to ask questions 
and receive understandable answers before making any decision.  
 
I understand that the record of my involvement in the research will be kept confidential. I have been informed that 
everything I say will be anonym ized. The event data will be recorded via paper notes/electronic notes/voice 
recorder/camera recorder4 and I understand that I can request a copy of these records to review if I wish. I understand 
that I am also allowed to delete or make any changes to these records if I feel the information I provided could be 
improved or clarified. I understand that information about my personal involvement in the research will be kept in a 
secure location at TELECOM ITALIA SPA and that my information will be made anonymous when shared with 5G-
SOLUTIONS project team. I understand that the data I provide will be anonymised and the record of my participation 
will be kept in a file separate from the project data. I understand that the data will be kept for one year after the 5G-
SOLUTIONS project ends, but my personal data will be destroyed when the project ends. 
 
I understand that this research conforms to European Commission guidelines and that it has been approved by the 
Ethics Committee in the Research Executive Agency managing Horizon 2020 projects. Finally, I have b een given 
the contact details of the research team and I have been informed that I am free to contact TELECOM ITALIA SPA 
(Project Coordinator) about any queries relating to my data or the project itself:
